<script>
  const my_utmParameters = [
    "gclid",
	"twclid",
    "rdt_cid",
    "cls",
    "utm_source",
    "utm_medium",
    "utm_campaign",
    "utm_term",
    "utm_content"
  ];

  function getAllUrlParams() {
    let obj = Object.fromEntries(new URLSearchParams(location.search));
    return obj;
  }

  var cookieExist = Cookies.get('Lead');
  var getAllUrlParamsObj = getAllUrlParams();
  var getAllUrlParamsJSON = JSON.stringify(getAllUrlParamsObj);
  var isEmpty = jQuery.isEmptyObject(getAllUrlParamsObj);

  if (!isEmpty && typeof cookieExist === 'undefined') {
    console.log("Case 1 - parameters & no cookie exist => Create Cookie");
    createLead();
    setUTMformValues();
  }

  let compare = is_this_utm_equal_to_cookie_utm_values();

  if (!isEmpty && typeof cookieExist !== 'undefined') {
    if (!compare) {
      Cookies.remove('Lead');
      createLead();
      setUTMformValues();
    } else {
      setUTMformValues();
    }
  }

  if (isEmpty && typeof cookieExist !== 'undefined') {
    setUTMformValues();
  }

  function createLead() {
    var lead = {
      parameters: getAllUrlParamsObj
    };
    Cookies.set('Lead', lead, { expires: 1 });
  }

  function is_this_utm_equal_to_cookie_utm_values() {
    if (typeof cookieExist === 'undefined') {
      return false;
    }

    for (const this_utm_element of my_utmParameters) {
      let value_exist = JSON.parse(cookieExist).parameters[this_utm_element] === getAllUrlParamsObj[this_utm_element];
      if (!value_exist) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  function setUTMformValues() {  
    const empty_param_case = "null";
    for (const this_utm_element of my_utmParameters) {
      set_utm_field(this_utm_element);
    }

    function set_utm_field(utm_type) {
      let utm_value = JSON.parse(Cookies.get('Lead')).parameters[utm_type];
      let utm_nodes = document.getElementsByClassName(utm_type);
      
      if (utm_nodes.length > 0) {
        for (var i = 0; i < utm_nodes.length; i++) {
          if (!!utm_value && utm_value !== undefined) {
            utm_nodes[i].value = utm_value;
          } else {
            utm_nodes[i].value = empty_param_case;
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
</script>

<script>
    window.addEventListener("load", function () {
        let splitWords = function (selector) {
            var elements = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
            elements.forEach(function (el) {
                el.dataset.splitText = el.textContent;
                el.innerHTML = el.textContent
                    .split(/\s/)
                    .map(function (word) {
                        return word
                            .split("-")
                            .map(function (word) {
                                return '<span class="word">' + word + "</span>";
                            })
                            .join('<span class="hyphen">-</span>');
                    })
                    .join('<span class="whitespace"> </span>');
            });
        };

        let splitLines = function (selector) {
            var elements = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
            splitWords(selector);
            elements.forEach(function (el) {
                var lines = getLines(el);

                var wrappedLines = "";
                lines.forEach(function (wordsArr) {
                    wrappedLines += '<span class="line"><span class="words">';
                    wordsArr.forEach(function (word) {
                        wrappedLines += word.outerHTML;
                    });
                    wrappedLines += "</span></span>";
                });
                el.innerHTML = wrappedLines;
            });
        };

        let getLines = function (el) {
            var lines = [];
            var line;
            var words = el.querySelectorAll("span");
            var lastTop;
            for (var i = 0; i < words.length; i++) {
                var word = words[i];
                if (word.offsetTop != lastTop) {
                    // Don't start with whitespace
                    if (!word.classList.contains("whitespace")) {
                        lastTop = word.offsetTop;

                        line = [];
                        lines.push(line);
                    }
                }
                line.push(word);
            }
            return lines;
        };

        splitLines(".reveal-text");

        let revealText = document.querySelectorAll(".reveal-text");

        gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
        let revealLines = revealText.forEach((element) => {
            const lines = element.querySelectorAll(".words");

            let tl = gsap.timeline({
                scrollTrigger: {
                    trigger: element,
                    toggleActions: "restart none none reset"
                }
            });
            tl.set(element, { autoAlpha: 1 });
            tl.from(lines, 1, {
                yPercent: -100,
                ease: Power3.out,
                stagger: 0.1,
                delay: 0.2
            });
        });
    });

</script>

<!-- phone number validation -->
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/libphonenumber-js@1/bundle/libphonenumber-min.js" data-airgap-id="21"></script>
<script>
    const DEFAULT_COUNTRY = 'US'
    const formatter = new libphonenumber.AsYouType(DEFAULT_COUNTRY)
    const phoneInput = document.getElementById('myphone')
    phoneInput.addEventListener('input', function (event) {
        formatter.reset()
        const newValue = formatter.input(phoneInput.value)
        phoneInput.value = newValue
        if (!libphonenumber.isValidPhoneNumber(newValue, DEFAULT_COUNTRY)) {
            phoneInput.setCustomValidity('Invalid phone number')
        } else {
            phoneInput.setCustomValidity('')
        }
    })
</script>













  <script>
  
  
  
  // Contact form Checkboxes in footer
  $(document).ready(function() {
        const $checkAllBox = $('#form-check-all');
        const $checkboxes = $('#checkbox-wrapper .w-checkbox-input:not(#form-check-all .w-checkbox-input)');
        const $checkLine = $('.form-checkbox-line:first');
        const $checkboxesParent = $('#checkbox-wrapper .form-checkbox:not(#form-check-all)');
    
        // If we've found some checkboxes
        if (!$checkAllBox.length || !$checkboxes.length) return;
    
        // If we checked an ALL checkbox
        $checkAllBox.on('click', function(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
  
         // Check for unchecked boxes 	
         const $uncheckedCheckboxes = $('#checkbox-wrapper .w-checkbox-input:not(.w--redirected-checked):not(#form-check-all .w-checkbox-input)');
  
          // If there's at least one unchecked box, check all
          if ($uncheckedCheckboxes.length > 0) {
              $checkboxes.addClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkAllBox.find('.w-checkbox-input').addClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkLine.hide();
              // Create checked state for JS manipulation
              $checkboxesParent.find('input').prop("checked", true);
          } else {
              // If all are checked, uncheck all
              $checkAllBox.find('.w-checkbox-input').removeClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkboxes.removeClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkLine.hide();
              $checkboxesParent.find('input').prop("checked", false);
          }
      });
      $checkboxesParent.on('click', function(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
          // Get all unchecked checkboxes
          const $uncheckedOtherCheckboxes = $('#checkbox-wrapper .w-checkbox-input:not(.w--redirected-checked):not(#form-check-all .w-checkbox-input)');
          // Check if the checkbox is checked
          if ($(this).find('.w--redirected-checked').length > 0) {
            // Uncheck this checkbox
            $(this).find('.w--redirected-checked').removeClass('w--redirected-checked');
            $(this).find('input').prop("checked", false);
            // Check if we have any other checkboxes left checked. First if not then:
            if (($uncheckedOtherCheckboxes.length + 1) == $checkboxes.length) {
              $checkAllBox.find('.w-checkbox-input').removeClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkLine.hide();
            } else {
              // Add minus symbol since not all are checked
              $checkAllBox.find('.w-checkbox-input').removeClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $checkLine.show();            
            }
  
          } else {
              // Check this checkbox and run tests
              $(this).find('.w-checkbox-input').addClass('w--redirected-checked');
              $(this).find('input').prop("checked", true);
              // Get all empty checkboxes
              const $allCurrentCheckboxes = $('#checkbox-wrapper .w-checkbox-input:not(.w--redirected-checked):not(#form-check-all .w-checkbox-input)');
              // Check how many checkboxes are checked
              if ($allCurrentCheckboxes.length == 0) {
                  // If all are checked now (besides the first one), check the first one
                  $checkAllBox.find('.w-checkbox-input').addClass('w--redirected-checked');
                  $checkLine.hide();
              }
          }
      });
  });
    
  
  
    
  </script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var emailField = document.querySelector('.hack18-email');

    if (emailField) {
      emailField.addEventListener('input', function () {
        var emailValue = emailField.value.toLowerCase();
        var blockedDomains = ['gmail.com', 'msn.com', 'hotmail.com', 'yopmail.com', 'mailinator.com', 'yahoo.com', 'outlook.com', 'icloud.com', 'qq.com', 'mail.com', 'proton.me', 'aol.com'];

        var isBlockedDomain = blockedDomains.some(function (domain) {
          return emailValue.includes(domain);
        });

        if (isBlockedDomain) {
          emailField.setCustomValidity('Please use your work email address');
        } else {
          emailField.setCustomValidity('');
        }
      });
    }
  });
</script>

<!-- Fâ€™in sweet Webflow Hacks for Nested Bullets -->
<script>
// when the DOM is ready
$(document).ready(function() {
  // get the li items
  const listItems = $('li');
  // for each li item
  listItems.each(function(index, item){
    // check for '~~~~' character
    // it's recommended to start with the deepest level of sub bullet
    // to ensure only the relevant classes are applied
    
    // if the li item text starts with '~~~~'
    if($(item).text().startsWith('~~~~')){
      // run indentText() function
      indentText(this, 'hack20-sub-bullet-4');
    }
    // else if the li item starts with '~~~'
    else if($(item).text().startsWith('~~~')){
      // run indentText() function
      indentText(this, 'hack20-sub-bullet-3');
    }	
    // else if the li item starts with '~~'
    else if($(item).text().startsWith('~~')){
      // run indentText() function
      indentText(this, 'hack20-sub-bullet-2');
    }	
    // else if the li item starts with '~'
    else if($(item).text().startsWith('~')){
      // run indentText() function
      indentText(this, 'hack20-sub-bullet');
    }	
  });
 
  // indentText function
  function indentText(li, className){
    // add relevant className to li item
    // if the li item text starts with '~~~~' add the sub-bullet-4 class
    // else if the li item starts with '~~~' add the sub-bullet-3 class
    // else if the li item starts with '~~' add the sub-bullet-2 class
    // else if the li item starts with '~' add the sub-bullet class
    $(li).addClass(className);
    // remove the '~' from the li items
    // the regex /~+/g 
    // matches any one or more ~ characters
    const reformatedText = $(li).html().replace(/~+/g,'');
    // replace the li item's html text that has ~ tags
    // with the new text that removed the ~ character(s)
    $(li).html(reformatedText);
  }
});
</script>

        var s = document.createElement('script'); s.type = 'text/javascript';
        s.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://' : 'http://') + piHostname + '/pd.js';
        var c = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; c.parentNode.insertBefore(s, c);
    }
    if(window.attachEvent) { window.attachEvent('onload', async_load); }
    else { window.addEventListener('load', async_load, false); }
})();
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/swiper@11/swiper-bundle.min.js" data-airgap-id="22"></script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    // Define the toggleArrows function
    function toggleArrows(swiper) {
      const prevArrow = document.querySelector(".testimonial-left-arrow");
      const nextArrow = document.querySelector(".testimonial-right-arrow");

      // Ensure arrows exist before applying logic
      if (prevArrow) {
        if (swiper.isBeginning) {
          prevArrow.classList.add("hide");
        } else {
          prevArrow.classList.remove("hide");
        }
      }

      if (nextArrow) {
        if (swiper.isEnd) {
          nextArrow.classList.add("hide");
        } else {
          nextArrow.classList.remove("hide");
        }
      }
    }

    // Initialize Primary Testimonials Slider
    const testimonialsSlider = new Swiper(".primary-testimonials--collection-list-wrapper", {
      wrapperClass: "primary-testimonials--collection-list", // Custom wrapper class
      slideClass: "swiper-slide", // Default slide class
      slidesPerView: 1,
      slidesPerGroup: 1,
      spaceBetween: 0, // Adjust spacing between slides
      navigation: {
        nextEl: ".testimonial-right-arrow",
        prevEl: ".testimonial-left-arrow",
      },
      breakpoints: {
        480: {
          slidesPerView: 1,
        },
        768: {
          slidesPerView: "auto",
        },
        992: {
          slidesPerView: "auto",
        },
      },
      on: {
        init: function () {
          toggleArrows(this); // Pass the Swiper instance to toggleArrows
        },
        slideChange: function () {
          toggleArrows(this); // Pass the Swiper instance to toggleArrows
        },
      },
    });

    // Initialize Featured Blog Slider
    const featuredBlogSlider = new Swiper(".featured-blog-slider", {
      direction: "horizontal",
      loop: false,
      slidesPerView: 1,
      slidesPerGroup: 1,

      },
      scrollbar: {
        el: ".swiper-scrollbar",
        draggable: true,
      },
    });
  });
